            (new Image).src = _G.lsUrl + '&Type=Event.ClientInst&DATA=[{"T":"CI.MetaError","FID":"CI","Name":"MetaJSError","Text":"' + escape(n) + '"}]'
        },
        getHref = function() {
            return location.href
        },
        regexEscape;
    try {
        regexEscape = function(n) {
            return n.replace(/([.?*+^$&[\]\\(){}|<>-])/g, "\\$1")
        };
        function jsErrorHandler(n) {
            var s,
                r,
                y,
                p,
                u,
                f,
                w,
                e,
                h,
                c,
                o;
            try {
                if (s = "ERC", r = window[s], r = r ? r + 1 : 1, r === 16 && (n = new Error("max errors reached")), r > 16)
                    return;
                window[s] = r;
                var l = n.error || n,
                    b = '"noMessage"',
                    k = n.filename,
                    d = n.lineno,
                    g = n.colno,
                    nt = n.extra,
                    a = l.severity || "Error",
                    tt = l.message || b,
                    i = l.stack,
                    t = '"' + escape(tt.replace(/"/g, "")) + '"',
                    it = new RegExp(regexEscape(getHref()), "g");
                if (i) {
                    for (y = /\(([^\)]+):[0-9]+:[0-9]+\)/g, u = {}; (p = y.exec(i)) !== null;)
                        f = p[1],
                        u[f] ? u[f]++ : u[f] = 1;
                    e = 0;
                    for (h in u)
                        u[h] > 1 && (c = regexEscape(h), w = new RegExp(c, "g"), i = i.replace(w, e), i += "#" + e + "=" + c, e++);
                    i = i.replace(it, "self").replace(/"/g, "");
                    t += ',"Stack":"' + (escape(i) + '"')
                }

                            开设的各种年卡、季卡、月卡、次卡都可以归类为基础护理类。基础护理的作用主要有两点：1、定期整理肌肤；2、放松享受。 定期整理肌肤 许多去
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            做 …

                        <h2>
                            <a target="_blank" href="https://www.chlitina.com.cn/" h="ID=SERP,5249.1">克丽缇娜</a>
                        </h2>
                    </div>
                    <div class="b_caption">
                        <div class="b_attribution" u="2|5236|4752115246628902|UZuCua43oUdxAwJH15cKVmu9X_Gwh0yk" tabindex="0">
                            <cite>https://www.chlitina.com.cn</cite>
                            <span class="c_tlbxTrg">
                                <span class="c_tlbxH" H="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" K="SERP,5250.1"></span>
                            </span>
                        </div>
                        <p class="b_lineclamp2 b_algoSlug">
                            <span class="algoSlug_icon" data-priority="2">网页</span>
                            克丽缇娜是一家以美容护肤保养品与
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            加盟为主，集研发、生产、销售为一体的知名企业。克丽缇娜进入中国大陆市场20年，近4500家
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            遍布全国33个省、自治区、直辖市，且加盟 …
                        </p>
                    </div>
                    <div class="pageRecoPlaceholder" data-tag="RelatedPageRecommendations.RecommendationsClickback"></div>
                </li>
                <li class="b_algo">
                    <div class="b_title">
                        <a target="_blank" class="sh_favicon" href="https://www.zhihu.com/topic/19666315" h="ID=SERP,5261.1">
                            <div class="wr_fav" data-priority="2">
                                <div class="cico siteicon" style="width:16px;height:16px;">
                                    <div class="rms_iac" style="height:16px;line-height:16px;width:16px;" data-height="16" data-width="16" data-alt="全球 Web 图标" data-role="presentation" data-class="rms_img" data-src="https://ts4.cn.mm.bing.net/th?id=ODLS.9882fc6b-c6e0-4e80-808f-2f15e1d990f0&amp;w=16&amp;h=16&amp;o=6&amp;pid=1.2"></div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </a>
                        <h2>
                            <a target="_blank" href="https://www.zhihu.com/topic/19666315" h="ID=SERP,5276.1">
                                <strong>美容院</strong>
                                 - 知乎
                            </a>
                        </h2>
                    </div>
                    <div class="b_caption b_stsp1">
                        <div class="b_attribution" u="3|5083|4511605662757159|Dt0b77ZtI5YDpGNFXU7zf7spwQF22LkP" tabindex="0">
                            <cite>https://www.zhihu.com/topic/19666315</cite>
                            <span class="c_tlbxTrg">
                                <span class="c_tlbxH" H="BASE:CACHEDPAGEDEFAULT" K="SERP,5277.1"></span>
                            </span>
                        </div>
                        <p class="b_lineclamp2 b_algoSlug">
                            <span class="algoSlug_icon" data-priority="2">网页</span>
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            是为人们提供美容护理、皮肤保健、水疗等内容的美容服务场所。从90年代兴起，经历了指导型
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            、养护型
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            、修复型
                            <strong>美容院</strong>
                            三个阶段，到目前为止，已经发展到了调理型美容 …
                        </p>

                                服务项目种类繁多，分类方法各不相同。按照护理的目的可分为美容类项目和养生类项目。美容类项目包括面部项目、身体项目。面部 …
                            </p>
